1b1(sna tshogs): //rgya gar skad du/An d+hiklam pa ra bo gra ba
1b2(sna tshogs): ta ni rje sha/bod skad du/'phags pa rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas
1b3(sna tshogs): ga gyu gyu ga/
1b4(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' dang rang rgyas dang nyan thos thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo//'di skad
2a1(sna tshogs): bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na/'od
2a2(sna tshogs): ma'i tshe la bya ka lan du ka gnas pa na/dge slong stong nyis brgya lde bcu'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po
2a3(sna tshogs): dang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/sangs rgyas kyi zhing tha dad pa nas 'dus pa/
2a4(sna tshogs): skye ba gcigo gis thogs pa/tshad med grangs med pa dang /thobs gcig tu bzhugs te/de'i
2a5(sna tshogs): tshe bcom ldan 'das 'khor brgya stong du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis bltas te chos ston to//
2b1(sna tshogs): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa zhes bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur nas
2b2(sna tshogs): 'dug pa de stan las langs te/bla gos phrag pa gcig tu bzur nas/pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sA la btsugs te/bcom
2b3(sna tshogs): ldan 'das ga la ba de log su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//gal te zhus nas zhu ba lung
2b4(sna tshogs): bstan pa'i slad/bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag la skabs phye na/de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
2b5(sna tshogs): rgyas la phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu lags so//de skad ceso gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis/byang chub sems dpa' sems
2b6(sna tshogs): dpa' chen po/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon bla 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/de
3a1(sna tshogs): /bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la khyod ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang /dris pad+ma
3a2(sna tshogs): dang de'i lung bstan pas khyod kyi sems rangs par bya'o//de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang /bcom ldan 'das la/byang chub sems dpa'
3a3(sna tshogs): sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pho rol tu phyin pa shes
3a4(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyid pa bcom ldan 'das ji tsam gyis na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol
3a5(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa zhes bgyi ba//bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa lags//
3a6(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin po la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
3b1(sna tshogs): bsgom pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba lags//bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa na
3b2(sna tshogs): bdud sdig can gyis glegs mi rnyed cing bdud kyi las thams cad kyang rtogs par 'gyur ba lags/bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes
3b3(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa ji lta bus gnas na myur du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi chos yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba lags/de skad ces gsol pa dang /
3b4(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par
3b5(sna tshogs): gnon po khyad byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi don dang /ci nas khyod skye bo mang po la phan pa dang /skye bo mang po la bde ba dang /'jig rten
3b6(sna tshogs): la snying btso ba dang /lha dang mi rnams kyi skye bo phal po che'i don dang /phan pa dang /bde ba'i phyir zhugs shing /da ltar gyi dang ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
3b7(sna tshogs): sems dpa' chen po rnams la snang ba byed par 'dod pas/de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la shos rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
4a1(sna tshogs): //pa 'dri ba legaso leg so//de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mkhyen bzhin du/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon
4a2(sna tshogs): pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa khyod don gyi dbang gang mthong nas de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di lta bu 'dri/de skad ces
4a3(sna tshogs): bka' stsal pa dang /bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan
4a4(sna tshogs): 'das sems can thams cad la smin pa dang /sems can thams cad la snying brtse ba dang /sems can thams cad kyi don gyi slad bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la ngan
4a5(sna tshogs): 'di zhu lags so//de ci'i slad du zhe na/bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni nyan thos dang /rang sangs rgyas dang /byang chub
4a6(sna tshogs): sems dpa' dang /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos dang /chos thams cad sdud pa logs pa'i slad du'o//bcom ldan 'das de la sems tsun gang dag
4a7(sna tshogs): nyan thos kyi theg pa la nges par gyur pa de dag gis thos ni myur du zag pa ma mchis pa'i sa mngon sum du bgyid par 'gyur ba dang /gang dag rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa
4b1(sna tshogs): la nges par gyur pa de dag kyang myur du rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pas nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang /gang dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la yang dag par zhugs pa de dag kyang myur du bla na mod pa
4b2(sna tshogs): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba dang /gang dag yang dag pa nyid skyon med pa la ma zhugs shing so gsum la ma nges pa de dag gis thos na bla na med pa yang dag
4b3(sna tshogs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par 'gyur ba dang /bcom lda 'das de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di zhus pa'i lan btab pas/sems can thad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba
4b4(sna tshogs): bskyed par 'gyur ba'i slad du/de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes bstan du gsol/bcom ldan 'das bdag ni sems can dman pa la mos pa rnams kyi slad du de
4b5(sna tshogs): bzhin gshegs pa la zhu ba ma lags/dbul ba'i sems dang ldan pa rnams kyi ma lags/dbul po'i theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/le lo can rnams
4b6(sna tshogs): kyi slad du ma lags/le lo'i zil gyis non pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/lta ba'i 'dam du bying ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/bdud kyi zhags pas zin pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/
4b7(sna tshogs): ngo tsha ma 'tshal cing khrel ma mchis pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/yo byad bsnyungs pa dang mi ldan pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/bskra dngas pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/
5a1(sna tshogs): sems 'khrul pa rnams kyi slad ma lags/'dod pa'i 'dam du bying ba rnams kyi slad ma lags/gal can rnams kyi sla du ma lags/sgyu can rnams kyi/
5a2(sna tshogs): sla du ma lags/bgyis pa mi bzo ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/sdig pa 'tshol ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags/sdig pa spyod pa rnams kyi sla ma lags/tshul
5a3(sna tshogs): khrims nyams pa rnams kyi sla du ma lags/tshul khrims yongs su ma dag pa rnams kyi sla du ma lags/lta ba ma nyams pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/bdud kyi//
5a4(sna tshogs): spyod yul la spyod pa rnams kyi sla du ma lags/bdag le bstod pa rnams kyi sla du ma lags/gzhan la smod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/rnyed pa dang bkur sti la
5a5(sna tshogs): gdu ba rnams kyi sla du ma lags/lhung bzed dang chos gos la chags pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/tshul 'chos pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/khwa gsag can rnams/
5a6(sna tshogs): kyi sla ma lags/gzhog slongs can rnams kyi slad du ma lags/thob kyis 'jal ba rnams kyi spya du ma lags/rnyed pa la rnyed par sgrub pa rnams kyi sladadu ma lags/
5a7(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das sems can de lta bu rnams kyi slad du bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu ba ma lagaso//bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
5b1(sna tshogs): /shos tshol ba dang /chags pa ma mchis pa'i ye shes dang /rang byung gi ye shes dang /mi mnyam bu'i ye shes dang /bla na med pa'i ye shos tshol ba de dag dang /gang dag bdag/
5b2(sna tshogs): dang pha rol kyang mi dmigs na/bdag la stod pa dang /gzhan la smod pa lta ga la mchis te/bcom ldan 'das rwa bcad pa lta bur nga rgyal ma mchis pa/zug rngu phyung
5b3(sna tshogs): gdol pa lta bur sems dma' ba/sems sa dang /chu dang /me dang /rlung dang /na mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i sems can rnams dang /byang chub sems dpa' sems
5b4(sna tshogs): dpa' chen po rnams kyi slad bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lagaso//bcom ldan 'das gang dag chos kyang mi dmigs shing rlom semasu mi bgyid la ma ngon par zhen pa ma mchis
5b5(sna tshogs): ni/chos mi lags pa lcu ga la mchis te/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi sgrung bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu ba lag so//bcom ldan 'das bsam
5b6(sna tshogs): pa dag pa/g.yo ma mchis pa/sgyu ma mchis pa/drang ba/sems mnyam pa/sems can thams cad la sman pa dang /snying brtse ba can yang dag par 'dzin du stsol ba/
5b7(sna tshogs): yang dag par gzeng bstod pa/yang dag par dga' bar bgyid pa/khur chen po khyer ba/zag pa chen po la mngon par zhugs pa/bgyi ba chen pos so sor nye bar gnas pa/
6a1(sna tshogs): snying chen po dang ldan pa/snyoms can thams cad 'dra ba thob par bgyid pa/'dron pa/rnam par 'dren pa/yongs su 'dren pa/chos thams nad la mi brtan//
6a2(sna tshogs): par gnas pa/skye ba'i gnas thams cad mi tshol ba/bdud kyi zhags pa thams cad las rnam par grol ba/'dun pa can brtson 'grus dang ldan pa/brag mchis pa/chos
6a3(sna tshogs): thams cad kyi dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa/the tshom thams cad gcod pa la mkhas pa'i sems can rnams dang /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi slad du
6a4(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lagaso//bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la yang rlom semasu mi bgyid cing mngon par mi
6a5(sna tshogs): zhen la chags par mi gnas shing /rlom sems thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i lam la gnas pa/lam du zhugs pa/lam ston pa'i sems can rnams
6a6(sna tshogs): dang /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi sladadu/bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lag so//bcom ldan 'das bdag ni sems
6a7(sna tshogs): can thams cad la bde ba dang /lhag na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang /bla na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang /mya ngan las 'das pa'i bde ba dang /sangs rgyas kyi bde ba dang /
6b1(sna tshogs): 'dus ma bgyes pa'i bde ba nye bar bsgrub par 'tshal te/bdag sems can thams cad kyi don dang /sman pa dang /bde ba dang /grub pa dang /bde ba'i slad du de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu
6b2(sna tshogs): lagaso//bcom ldan 'das bdag ni the tshom ma mchis par 'tshal zhing /the tshom mchis nas kyang sems can rnams kyi the tshom rab tu spong ba'i slad chos bshad par 'tshal te
6b3(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das bdag sems can thams cad kyi tha tshom bsal ba'i sla du bcom ldan 'das la zhu lagaso//de ci'i sladadu zhe na/bcom ldan 'das sems can thams cad ni sdug bsngal/
6b4(sna tshogs): rang mi mthun zhing bde ba 'tshal la/sems can thams cad ni bde ba don du gnyer ba lags te/bcom ldan 'das shes rab ma gtogs par gzhan sems can rnams kyi bde ba
6b5(sna tshogs): gang yang bdag gis ma mthong zhing /bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa/theg pa chen po ma gtogs par sems can rnams kyi bde ba gang yang ma mchis te/bcom
6b6(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bdag gis don gyi dbang 'di mthong bas semaso can rnams la bde ba nye bar bsgrubs pa'i slad du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhu lagaso//bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems
6b7(sna tshogs): dpa' rnams kyi don 'di yang dag par mthong bas bdag gi de bzhin gshegs pa la doni 'di zhu lags so//de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems
7a1(sna tshogs): dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bku' stsal to//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa leg sngo lpagaso//khyad skye'o//
7a2(sna tshogs): phal po che la snying brtse ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di 'dri ba ni khyod kyi yon tan gyi mtha' rtogs par sla ba ma yino//de'i phyir rab kyi rtsal gyis
7a3(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa legs par nyon la yid la rab tu zung shig dang /ngas khyod la bshad//bcom ldan 'das leg so zhes gsol nas/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
7a4(sna tshogs): chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa bcom ldan 'das kyi ltar nyan po dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
7a5(sna tshogs): khyod 'di skadadu/bcom ldan 'das khyod shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi ba bcom ldan 'das ji tsam gyis na/byang chub sems dpa' rnam
7a6(sna tshogs): kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi zhes zer ba ni rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni chos gang gis kyang brjod par bya ba ma yin te/shA
7a7(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshig thams cad las blangs pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/'di shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//
7b1(sna tshogs): 'ad+mo/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhes brjod par myo nus//rab kyi rtsalA gyis rnam par gnon pa 'di ni chos thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin
7b2(sna tshogs): pa yin te/de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rgyal gyis rnam par gnon pa/shes rab nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pas ma rnyed ma dmigs na shes ra
7b3(sna tshogs): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lta dmigs par ga la 'gyur/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab ces bya ba 'di ni chos thams cad kun du shes pa 'di ni chos thams cad kun tu rig pa
7b4(sna tshogs): ste de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/chos thams cad kun tu rig pa gong zhes na/chos 'di dag thams cad ni rnam pa gzhan na chos thams cad
7b5(sna tshogs): rnam pa gzhan du brjod de/chos thams cad ni brjod pa las rnam par grol ba ma yino//gang chos thams cad kun tu shes pa dang /gang chos thams cad rkun tu rig pa de yang
7b6(sna tshogs): tshig gis brjed par mi nus mod kyi/'on kyang ji ltar sems can rnams kyis shes par 'gyur ba de ltar shes rab ces bya'o//'di ni btags pa zhes bya ste/de'i phyir shes rab ces
7b7(sna tshogs): bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/chos thams cad ni gdag su med/gzung du med/bshad du mod/snang ba med/de lta bur kun du rig pa de ni kun du rig pa rje
8a1(sna tshogs): bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab ces bya ba de ni shes pa'ang ma yin kun tu mi shes pa'ang ma yin de las kyang mA yin de la snga ma yin pa yang ma
8a2(sna tshogs): yin te de'i phyir shwe rab ces bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de ni mi shes pa'i spyod yul yang ma yin/ye shes kyi spyod yul yang ma yin/mi shes pa'i yul yang //
8a3(sna tshogs): mA yin/ye shes kyi yul yang ma yin te/ye shes ni yul med pa'o//gal te ye shes la yul yod du zin nu mi shes par 'gyuraro//ye shes ni mi shes pa las ma
8a4(sna tshogs): yin/mi shes pa'ang ye shes las ma yin/ye shes ni mi shes pa ma yin/ye shes pa yang ye shes ma yin te/ye shes kyis ye shes shes bya'o//ye shes
8a5(sna tshogs): kyis mi shes pa zhes bya'o//mi shes pas ye shes shes bya'o//de la ye shes de ni 'di'o//ye shes de ni 'di'i'o//ye shes de ni 'diso//ye shes de ni 'di'i phyir ro zhe
8a6(sna tshogs): ye shes cung zad kyang bstan par mi nus te/de'i phyir ye shes de ni ye shes nyid kyis medo//ye shes kyang ye shesu mi gnas te/mi shes pas kyang ye shes shes mi bya'o//
8a7(sna tshogs): gal te mi shes pas ye shes shes bya na ni/de'i phyir byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyang ye shes can du 'gyuraro//gang ye shes dang mi shes pa mi dmigs shing ye shes
8b1(sna tshogs): dang mi shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa de nyid ye shes shes bya ste/yo shos ni ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du ma yin no//dro bas na yA shas nI brjod par bya ba
8b2(sna tshogs): ma yin zhing /yul thams cad las rab tu 'das pa ste/ye shes ni glang gi yul yang ma yino//ye shes kyi yul yang gang yang ma yi no//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par
8b3(sna tshogs): gnon pa/ye shes bstan pa'i yul yang ma yin/phyogs kyang ma yin pa 'di gang gis shes pa de ni ye shes can nam ye shes can ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su mi 'gro'o//
8b4(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gang 'di ltar rab tu shes pa dang rje su rtogs pa dang kun tu shes pa de ni shes rab ces bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gang
8b5(sna tshogs): 'di ltar mngon par rtogs pa mngon sum du byed pa de ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o//'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces ji skad brjod pa bzhin du ni ma
8b6(sna tshogs): yin//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'jig rten nyid kyang mi dmigs na 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab lta ga la yod/'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab kyis gang 'jig rten lngas sgrol
8b7(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur ba lta ci smos/de ci'i phyir zhe na/des 'jig rten mi dmigs pas ci yang sgrol bar mi byed de/de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o//rab kyi rtsal
9a1(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa 'jig rten zhes bya ba 'di ni btags pa zhes brjod pa ste/btags pa ni 'jig rten las yang drag par 'dras pa ma yin gyi/btags pa thaMd/
9a2(sna tshogs): las yang dag par 'das pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o//'da' bar bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ma yin gyi 'da' bar mi bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'o//de ci'i
9a3(sna tshogs): phyir zhe na/de la gang 'da' bar bya ba dang /gang gis 'do' bar bya ba'i chos phra rab tsam yang med pas de'i phyir 'das pa zhes bya ste/'jig rten las 'das pa la ni 'jig rten
9a4(sna tshogs): yang med/'jig rten las 'das pa yang med//bla na med pa la ni bsgral ba med/de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
9a5(sna tshogs): 'di ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab bstan pa zhes bya ste/'jig rten 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yino//de ci'i phyir zhe na//
9a6(sna tshogs): 'jig rten las 'das pa ni brjod par bya ba ma yin gyi do ni brgal ba ste/de la ni 'da' bar bya ba ci yang med pas de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o//
9a7(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de lo gang nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab des ci nges par rtogs/'di la ni nges par rtogs par bya ba ci yang medado//gal te nges par rto/
9b1(sna tshogs): par bya ba 'ga' zhes yod du zin na ni 'di shes rab kyis nges par rtogs pa zhes gdags na gang gis kyang mi rtogs shing /kun rtogs pa ma yin la/gang gis rtogs par 'gyur
9b2(sna tshogs): pa'i bye phrag gang yang mi dmigaso//nges par rtogs pa zhes bya ba ni 'di la rtogs par byed pa ci yang med cing kun tu rtogs par bya ba yang med/de la rtogs par byed pa ci yang med
9b3(sna tshogs): cing kun tu rtogs par bya ba yang med pas de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhes bya'o//'di lnga ni gang yang mthar 'gro ba med cing dpung du yang ma yin te/de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhe
9b4(sna tshogs): bya'o//nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis rtogs pa ni steng ma rtogs te/gang du yang mi rgyug rnam par mi rgyug la/kun tu mi rgyug ste/de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhes bya'o//

12a1(sna tshogs): phyir 'byung ba dang nub pa rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya ba de ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yongs su shes pa/

12a3(sna tshogs): gnon pa de ni rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba bzhin du skye ba med par bstan to//mi skye ba ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ste/mi 'byung ba mnyam pas de

12a6(sna tshogs): do ltar byung ba ma yin/gang 'das pa ma yin/ma 'ongs pa ma yin/da ltar byung ba ma yin pa de la 'gog pa medado//grung la 'gog pa med pa de ni mi skye ba she bra nas
12a7(sna tshogs): bya'o//gang gis mi skye bar shes pa de ni yang bskyed pa ma yin/'gog pa mngon sum du byed pa'ang ma yin//gang mi skye ba de 'gog pa mi byed/skye ba yin na ni/

13a1(sna tshogs): tau/rab kyi rgyal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gang gis chos thams cad mi zad pa dang /zad pA shes pA lA brtags pa khong du chud pa de zad pa shes pa dang bral ta/

13a4(sna tshogs): pa brjod par bya ba ma yin pa ste/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings bstan pa 'di yang ji skad bstan pa bzhin du ni ma yino//bstan pa

13b2(sna tshogs): tshu la 'am bA ro'i dmigs na ni de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshu rol 'am pha rol bshad pa zhig ni/rab kyi rgyal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rob

13b6(sna tshogs): du chu de mi 'ga'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/de la khang du chud pa ci yang med cing rab tu rtogs pa yang med pa'i phyir//khong du chud pa dang /rab tu rtogs pa mnyam pa nyid ni byang

14a7(sna tshogs): nam sems can du gdags pa med pa de la 'di byang chub sems dpa' 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes ji ltar brjod/rab kyi rtsal gyis

16a1(sna tshogs): de ltar cho snga thams cad khong du chud pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams bri ba med cing gang ba med pa'o//chos thams cad bro ba med cing gAng du med pa'i phyir spangs/

16a5(sna tshogs): ne tha dad du mi dmig so//sems can gyi khams dang chos kyi dbyings bri ba 'am gang ba dmigs pa 'am yod pa ma yin te/gang gis de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces

16b1(sna tshogs): ces bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa byang chub ces bya ba de ni sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyi //sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid ji lta bu zhe na/chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid
16b2(sna tshogs): mtshan nyid med pa de ni sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyido//byang chub ni mtshan nyid med pa ste mtshan nyid kyi rang bzhin la so bzlog pa'o//gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces
16b3(sna tshogs): bya ste/ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de ni chos thams cad rjesu rtogs pas byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal//

16b5(sna tshogs): de ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams ring //de ni byang chub sems dpa'i ming gis lho dang mi dang lha ma yin dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la slu ba'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis
16b6(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa gal te tshig tsam gyis byang chub sems dpar gyur na ni/dri'i phyir sems can thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpar 'gyuraro//rab kyi rtsal gyis
16b7(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa/'di lta ste byang chubo sems dpa'i sa zhes bya ba de ni tshig gi las tsam ma yin//tshig gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang
17a1(sna tshogs): chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nu so//tshig gri las kyis byang chub dang byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams thob par mi 'gyuraro//rab kyi rdul gyis
17a2(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa sems can thams cad ni byang chub la spyod mod kyi/mi shes shing khong du ma chudade/de'i phyir de dag byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/
17a3(sna tshogs): sems can rnams sems can med par mi shes pa'i phyir ro//gal te de ltar shes na bdag gi spyod pa dag gis byang chub sems dpa' dag tu 'gyur ba'i rig so//sems
17a4(sna tshogs): can thams cad ni phyin ci log pas rang gi spyod pa dang /rang gi yul dang rang gi spyod yul rab tu mo sheso//gaul ti rang gi spyod pa rab tu shes na ni/de dag slar gang la
17a5(sna tshogs): yang rnam par rtog cing spyod par mi 'gyuraro//rnam par rtog pa dang spyod pa de dag gis byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad yang dag pa ma yin pa la dmigs shing spyod kyang de dag
17a6(sna tshogs): byang chub la dmigs po snyam du rlom sems su byed/dmigs po la spyod cing rtog pa la spyod pa de dag la byang chub ga la yod/byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams grwa
17a7(sna tshogs): lo yod/gang gi chos de lta bur rab tu shes pa de dag slar yang dag po ma yin pa'i dmig pa la mi spyod cing de dag ni phyir chos gang yang rlom sem su mi byed/de'i
17b1(sna tshogs): phyir spyod pa med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa zhes bya'o//byang chub sems dpa' ni rtog pa dang rnam par rtog pa la mi spyod//gang la rtog pa med pa de la spyod pa gang yang mdo//
17b2(sna tshogs): gong la rnam par rtog pa med pa de la spyod pa'i drin gang yong mdo//sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod po thams cad ni rnam par mi rtog par spyod cing thams cad rlom
17b3(sna tshogs): sems med la dmigs pa dang bcas pa ma yin pa ste/chos thams cad de ltar rab tu shes pa de ni phyir dmigs po 'am rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa 'am rnam par spyod pa med//de
17b4(sna tshogs): ni sdod pa med pa'i tshul gyis byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de ltar na byang chub semaso dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
17b5(sna tshogs): la spyod pa yino//rab kyi rtsol gyis rnam par gnon pa gang de ltar chos khong du chud cing rab tu rtogs pa de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o//des sems can du 'du shes//
17b6(sna tshogs): pa bsal bas sems can med pa zhes bya ba de ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshig bla dgas so//de ci'i phyir zhe na/des sems can thams cad yang dag pa ma yin pa dang /saM naM
17b7(sna tshogs): thams cad sems can ma yin pa dang /sems can thams cad ni phyin ci log gis sems can dang /sems can thams cad ni yongasu brtogs pas sems can dang /sems
18a1(sna tshogs): can thams cad ni yod pa ma yin pa la dmigs pas sems can dang /sems can thams cad ni rang gi spyod pa rnam par ma rung bar byas pas sems can dang /sems
18a2(sna tshogs): can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can zhes shes pa'i phyir//de ci'i phyir zhe na/sems can thams cad ni chos gang dag med pa'i chos de dag mngon par 'du byed pas
18a3(sna tshogs): de'i phyir sems can thams cad ni mi rig pa 'du byed pas sems can zhes bya'o//chos med pa gang zhe na/de na 'am/nga'i zhe 'am/nga'o zhes bya ba'i chos gang yang med pa'o//
18a4(sna tshogs): galho te chos 'ga' zhig du zhe 'am pa'i zhe 'am/nga'o zhes bya bar gyur na de'i phyir sems can thams cad yang dag par 'gyur ba zhig na/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
18a5(sna tshogs): 'di ltar nga zhe 'am/nga'i zhe 'am/nga'o zhes bya ba'i chos gong yang med pas de'i phyir sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa ste/sems can thams cad ni mi rig pa 'du byed
18a6(sna tshogs): pas sems can thams cad ces bya'o//rab kyi skyil gyis rnam par gnan pa/gong la yang nga zhi 'am/nga'i zhe'am/nga'o zhes bya ba'i sems can zhes bya ba'i chos
18a7(sna tshogs): yang med/gang gi phyir med pa de'i sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o//yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba de ni sems can med pa'i tshig bla dgas so//ji ltar rin
18b1(sna tshogs): du 'du shes pa yang dag pa ma yin pa la mngon par zhen pa de ltar sems can rnams yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya//
18b2(sna tshogs): pade lnga ni yang dag pa ci yang med cing ma byung ba'o//chos thams cad kyang yang dag pa ma yin zhing ma byung ba'o//de la sems can yang dag pa ma yin pa la lhag par chags pa de ni rnam
18b3(sna tshogs): par 'ching ba ste/de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa la dmigs pa ni sems can zhes bya'o//de dag ni skyod pa gang khang du chud pas byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba'i rang gi spyod
18b4(sna tshogs): pa de mi shes te/yongasu mi rtogs pas sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang de ltar tshwas khong du chud pa de ni byang chub sems
18b5(sna tshogs): dpa' zhes bya'o//byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba de ni gang gis chos thams cad khong du chud cing shes la/sems can rje su rtog pa'i tshig bla dgas so//ji ltar shes
18b6(sna tshogs): na/yang dag pa ma yin pa dang /ma byung ba dang /phyin ci log ma yin pa ro//ji ltar byis pa so so'i skye bo dag gis brtags pa de dag ni dri bzhin du ma yin no//ji ltar
18b7(sna tshogs): byis pa so so'i skye bo dag gis rnyed pa de dag de bzhin du ma yin te/de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/byang chub ni ma brtags rnam par ma brtags
19a1(sna tshogs): shing byang chub mngon pa ma bsgrubs lha mI dmigs pa'i phyid//rab kyi rnalnga gyis rnam par gnon pa/de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub mu bAn+tis+ho//chos
19a2(sna tshogs): thams cad mi rjed cing chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i phyir byang chub ces bya'o//de lta bu ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub ces bya ste/ji skad brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yino//rab
19a3(sna tshogs): kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag byang chub kyi phyir soms 'di bskyod par bya'o//zhes byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang /gang du bdag gis sems bskyed par bya ba'i
19a4(sna tshogs): byang chub de yod zhes byang chub rlom sem su byed pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa'o zhes mi bya ste/de dag ni sems can skyed pa zhes bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/'di ltar de dag
19a5(sna tshogs): ni skye bar mngon par mngon par zhen cing sems su mngon par zhen nas byang chub la mngon par zhen pa'i phyir//gang dag byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyod pa de dag ni byang chub kyi
19a6(sna tshogs): sems la mngon par zhen pa zhes bya'o//gang gi phyir mngon par 'du byed pa de'i phyir byang chub tu sems bskyed/de bsngo na mngon por 'du byed ni sems can zhes bya ste/byang //
19a7(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' ma yino//do ci'i phyir zhe na/de dag ni sems can skyes po zhes bya ba'i phyir//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/byang chub ni mi skyes shing /
19b1(sna tshogs): byang chub ni bsam du med pas byang chub kyi phyir de sbas par yi nus//rab kyi rtul gyis rnam par gnon pa de dag skye ba nyid la mngon par zhen kyang de dgra skye ba rab tu mi shes so//rab kyi rtsal
19b2(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa skye ba mo nyam pa nyid gang yin pa de ni ying dag pa nyid//sems mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa dang /yang dag pa nyid gang yon pa dang /mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa
19b3(sna tshogs): dang /yang dag pa nyid de ni byang chub ste/gang na yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid yod pa de na rnam par rtog pa gang yang med na de dag ni sems dang byang chub la rnam par brtags te/gnyisu
19b4(sna tshogs): mngon par zhen nas byang chub kyi phyir soms bskyed//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa sems kyang gzhan ma yin byang chub kyang gzhan ma yin/sems la byang chub med
19b5(sna tshogs): byang chub la yang sems med/byang chub gong yin pa dang /sems gang yin pa de ni yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhi no//de la ni byang chub kyang med/sems kyang maud//gang gis
19b6(sna tshogs): sems nyid dang /byang chub dang /skye ba dang /mi skye ba yang mi dmigs pa de byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o//yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems dpa' zhes bya'o//
19b7(sna tshogs): dpa' chen po zhes bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/des yong dag pa ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes pa'i phyir//yang dag pa ma yin pa gang zhe na/'jig rten thams cad ni yang
20a1(sna tshogs): dag pa ma yin pa ste/yang dag pa ma yin par rtogasaso//kye ma 'jig rten gnas pa 'di ni yang dag phra ma yin pa'o//ma byung ba'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/yung
20a2(sna tshogs): dag pa ma yin pa mi 'byung ba zhes bya zhe na/yang dag pa ma yin pa la 'byung ba gang yang med/yang dag pa ma yin pa ni mi 'byung ba'o//de'i phyir chos thams cad ni ngo
20a3(sna tshogs): pa nyid kyis med pa yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o//gang gis de ltar shes pa de ni yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems can zhes bya'o//yang dag pa la yang dag pa zhes
20a4(sna tshogs): mngon par mi zhen pas de'i phyir yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems can zhes bya ste/ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin//de ci'i phyir zhe na/yang dag pa ma yin pa
20a5(sna tshogs): la sems can nam sems tson+da chen po zhes bya ba gang yang med pa'i phyiraro//gong gis theg pa chen po khong du chud pa de sems can chen po zhes bya'o//theg pa chen po gang
20a6(sna tshogs): zhe na/thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ni thog pa chen po'o//thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes gang zhe na/gang ci yang rung ste 'dus byas shes pa dang /'dus ma byas
20a7(sna tshogs): shes pa dang /'jig rton shes pa dang /'jig rten las 'das pa shes pa des sems can chen po zhes bya'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/de sems can du 'du shes pa tshon
20b1(sna tshogs): po med pas de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o//de la ma rig pa'i phung po chen po med pas de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o//de la 'du byed kyi phung po med pas de'i phyir sems
20b2(sna tshogs): can chen po zhes bya'o//de la mi shes pa'i phung po chen po med pas de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o//de lnga sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po med pas de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes
20b3(sna tshogs): bya'o//rab kyi rtsol gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag sems chen po'o 'du shes la yang smod la sems kyang mi dmigs sems las byung ba'i chos dang sems kyi rang bzhin yang
20b4(sna tshogs): tu mi shes/byang chub kyang mi dmigs/byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams dang byang chub kyi rang bzhin yang rab tu mi shes te/de dag mi shes pa'i sems kyis byang chub kyang
20b5(sna tshogs): mi mthong /byang chub ma gtogs par sems kyang mi mthong /byang chub la sems mi mthong /sems la byang chub mi mthong ste/gang de ltar rnam par 'jig pa de ni sgom
20b6(sna tshogs): pa yang med/rnam par 'jig par byed pa yang med/de rnam par 'jig par byed pa de yang mi dmigs shing rlo mo sems su mi byed la/mngon par zhen pa de dag byang chub
20b7(sna tshogs): sems bskyed//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gang de ltar byang chub tu sems bskyed pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya ste/de dog bong chub
21a1(sna tshogs): las phyir mi ldog go//de ci'i phyir zhe na/gang dag 'di ltar byang chub dang sems dang skye ba dang /'gog pa tha dad du bya bar yang dag par rje su mi mthong ba de dag
21a2(sna tshogs): byang chub nyid la gnas pa ste/'di ni gang yong yang dag par rje su mi mthong //gang la yang mngon par mi zhe na/gang la yang rnam par rtog par mi 'gyur te/rab
21a3(sna tshogs): rtsol gyis rnam par gnon pa/gang dag de ltar rnam par grol ba dang /rnam par grol bar sems mi bskyed pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi
21a4(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag sems can du 'du shes pa dang /byang chub tu 'du shes pa dang /byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed na de dag ni byang chub las ring ba ste
21a5(sna tshogs): de ni byang chub dang nye ba ma yino//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag byang chub las ring ba 'am/nye bar yang dag par rjesu mi mthong ba de dag byang chub dang nye ba ste/
21a6(sna tshogs): de ni byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa ngos de la dgongs nas gang bdag gnyisu med par shes pa de ni sangs rgyas dang chos kyang rab tu
21a7(sna tshogs): shas zhes bshad//de ci'i phyir zhe na/gnyisu med par yong su shes pas chos thams cad yongasu shes te/de chos thams cad kyi bdag gi ngo bo nyid bsgom pa'i phyiraro//gang
21b1(sna tshogs): gnyi su med pa'i chos shes pa de ni sangs rgyas kyi chos shes pa ste/chos gnyi su med par yong su shes pas sangs rgyas kyi chos yongasu sheso//bdag yongasu shes phra khams gsuM
21b2(sna tshogs): thams cad yongasu sheso//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag yongasu shes pa zhes bya ba de ni chos thams cad kyi pha rolo//chos thams cad kyi pha rol yang gang zhe na
21b3(sna tshogs): gang pha rol nyid kyang mi dmigs/pha rol tu rlom sems su mi byed/pha rol la mngon par mi zhen pa de ni yongs su shes pas pha rol tu song ba zhes bya ste/ji skad du brjod pa
21b4(sna tshogs): bzhin du ni ma yino//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de lhor 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa yin par rig par bya'o//gang la shes par bya ba dang /rtogs par bya ba phra
21b5(sna tshogs): rab tsam yang med pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste de la ni 'ong ba 'am 'gro ba mi mngon no//gleng gzhi'i le'u zhes bya ste dang po'o///
21b6(sna tshogs): bam po gnyis pa/de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das nga rgyal can mtshan ma la spyod pa rnams
21b7(sna tshogs): brlan pa 'di la skrag par 'gyur lagaso//de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces smraso//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo 'di ni nga
22a1(sna tshogs): rgyal can rnams kyi yulA ma yon rtogs pa ma yin pas de dag 'di la skrag par mi 'gyur//de ci'i phyir zhe na/gang sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu song byed dag
22a2(sna tshogs): ni 'di la skrag par gyur zin pas 'di ni de dag gi yul mu yin zhing mi rtogs//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo gang dag nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir zhugs shing ngu rgyal spong ba'i phyir
22a3(sna tshogs): brtson pa de dag ni 'di la skrag par 'gyuraro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/nga rgyal yongs su shes pas nga rgyu la med pa tshal zhing nga rgyu la spong ba tshol ba'i phyiraro//tshe dang ldan pa
22a4(sna tshogs): kun dga' bo gang dag nga rgyal mi dmigs shing /yang dag par mi mthong la/rlom semasu mi byed cing mngon par mi zhon pa dri dag ni gang yong mi skrag gang la yang
22a5(sna tshogs): mi dngang gang la yang dngang par mi 'gyuraro//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo nga rgyal can rnams kyi phyir chusau bstan pa 'di zhugs pa ma yin//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo 'di/
22a6(sna tshogs): ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi yul ma yin te/go skabs med//gang dag nga rgyal spyad pa'i phyir brtson zhing 'bad pa de dag ni yang dag par 'bud pa ma yin//tshe dang ldan pa
22a7(sna tshogs): kun dga' bo nga rgyal zhes bya ba de ni lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs pa'i tshig blo dag so//gang dag nga rgyal la spyad cing lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs par byed pa de dag ni
22b1(sna tshogs): tshungs par mi spyod do//mtshungs par spyod pa yang chos 'di la the tshom za'o//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo gang dag mnyam pa yang mAM dmigs/mi mnyam pa spang ma
22b2(sna tshogs): yin/mnyam par yang rlom sems mi byed/mi mnyam par yang ma yin/mnyam par yAng mo zhe na/mi mnyam byar yang ma yin pa de dag ni gang la yang mi skrag
22b3(sna tshogs): mI dang dngang bar mi 'gyuraro//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo 'di ni byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyi yul ma yin te mi rtog so//tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo 'di ni byis pas
22b4(sna tshogs): sna'i skye bo thams cad kyis shes shing rtogs pa ma yin//tshe dang ldan pa kun dgo' bo nyan thos kyi theg pa can rnams kyis kyang mi rtogs//'di ni gang rang sangs rgyas
22b5(sna tshogs): kyi theg pa can chos zab mo la spyod pa de drug gis kyang mi rtog so/tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can gang dgra mtshan ma lA spyod pa dge ba'i
22b6(sna tshogs): bshes gnyen gyis yongs su mi zin pa sdig pa'i grogs pa'i lag tu seng ba de dag kyang chu gos pa med pa'i chos 'di dag mi rtogs shing yul ma yin te/tshe dang
22b7(sna tshogs): ldan pa kun dga' ba nyan thos kyi theg pa can bden pa mthong ba dang /byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi bstan pa/chos zab me la mos
23a1(sna tshogs): pa/gang chos 'di dag la mthun par spyod pa dang /gang chos 'di khyod du chud cing spyod pa rnams ni ma gtogs//kun dga' bo byang chub sems dpa mtshan ma//
23a2(sna tshogs): dang bral ba/mtshan ma med pa la spyod pa/sna tshogs med pa la spyod pa/zab mo'i cho sa shin tu ma thad phyin du/gang dag sems da byang chub kyang mi dmigs shing ches gang
23a3(sna tshogs): meng tha dad du mi byed la/yang dge pad+ma rje suM mi mthong ba de dag ni 'di lta bu'i chos la rmongs par mi 'byor the tshom mi za'o//de ci'i byod na ni/de dag chos thams cad
23a4(sna tshogs): rjesu mthun par gnas te mi mthun par ma yin pa'i phyir//de dag gis gang dang gang la chos 'dri ba de dang des rje su mthun par len 'debs shing d+hA su mthun par smra bar byed de//
23a5(sna tshogs): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//kun dga' ba ji ltar shA ri'i bu 'dis bshad pa de de bzhin te/kun dga' bo chos
23a6(sna tshogs): bstan pa 'di dang /sangs rgyas kyi byang chub dang rje su mthun pa'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub 'di ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi sa ma yin 'jug pa'i yul ma yin te/kun dga' bo
23a7(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya chen po la ni dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems mi 'jug/kun dga' bo dman pa la mos pa nga rgyal can rnams ni nga rgyal gyi dbang
23b1(sna tshogs): gis 'gro bas de dag sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la mi mthun par gnas//kun dga' bo 'khor 'di ni gcod ma ste/sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams la bya ba byas shing dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/
23b2(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen gyur byos pa/zab mo la mos pa zab mo spyod pa ste/kun dga' bo 'khor 'di la de bzhin gshegs pas yid brtan nas chos mngon par skyon gyi
23b3(sna tshogs): bsrung ba'i chus ni cung zad kyang mi ston to//kun dga' bo 'khor 'din snying po ste/seM zhag dang /gseg ma dang /gyo mo med pa/sangs rgyas brgya stong mad pa la baisbyin bgu
23b4(sna tshogs): byas pa/snying po la rab tu gnas pa'o//kun dga' bo gseg ma dang gyi me zhes bya ba de ni byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyi tshig bla dgas te/gang dag chos 'di la go skabs
23b5(sna tshogs): med pa'o//kun dga' bos zhag ces bya ba de ni sems can du rgyal can rnams kyi chog bla dgoso//kun+da dga' bo 'khor 'dri na nga rgyal med pa/dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos mngon
23b6(sna tshogs): par 'phags pa'i//kun dga' bo 'di lta ste dper na//klu'i rgyal ba mi dros pa rab tu dga' bar gyur te/dga' ba dang yid bde ba skyes nas rang gi gnas na 'dod pa'i ston
23b7(sna tshogs): lnga la kun du spyod cing rang gi gnas na rab tu dga' bar yan log brgyad dang ldan pa'i tshar gyi chu chen po 'bab so//de'i bur gyur pa de dog kyang rab tu dga' nas rang ring gi gnas
24a1(sna tshogs): na 'dod pa'i yon lnga 'byor cing ldan par gyur te/rtse zhing chung chen po 'bab so//kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshogs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
24a2(sna tshogs): rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang chos kyi cher chen po 'bebaso//gang 'di sras thu bo byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams 'di nas rang rang gi
24a3(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas kyi zhing du song ste/chos kun 'byung ba 'di la brtsams nas de bzhin poshegs pa de dag gi spyan sngar chos kyi char chen po gtong zhing chos kyi char chen po rab tu'i 'bru
24a4(sna tshogs): so//kun dga' bo 'di lta ste dper na klu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho ni gang gi tshe rab tu dga' bar gyur pa de'i tshe rang gi gnas nas char gyi rgyun chen po 'bab so//gang dag gnas don
24a5(sna tshogs): gnas par gyur pa'i klu de dag gis kyang cher gyi rgyun de mnos nas dga' bar gyur te char gyi rgyun des bde bar sheso//gang dag dri'i bur gyur pa de dag kyang char gyi rgyun de
24a6(sna tshogs): bzod cing char gyi rgyun des mchog tu dga' ba thob bo//de ci'i phyir zhe na/kun dga' bo klu gzhan dag gis char gyi rgyun de mi bzod la klu gzhan dag gis char gyi rgyun
24a7(sna tshogs): des bde bar mi shes shing char gyi rgyun dag gis dga' bar mi 'gyur ba'i phyir//kun dga' bo de bzhin du gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos dkon mchog la lhag
24b1(sna tshogs): par chags pa dang /glang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras kyi thu bo byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba byas pa bsam pa rgya che ba chos zab ma'i tshul las nges
24b2(sna tshogs): par skyes pa de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi tshul gyi char tshon po 'di bzod//thos nas rab tu dga' zhing mgu ste bde b.rasheso//kun dga' bo de bzhin gshegs
24b3(sna tshogs): pas don gyi dbang 'di la brten te bsam pa dag pa'i 'khor du seng ge'i sgra chen po sgrags cing chos kyi tshur chen po 'bebs so//kun dga' bo 'di lta ste dper na 'khor los bsgyur
24b4(sna tshogs): pa'i rgyal po rin po che'i mdzod mang po bsags pa dang ldan pa des bu mang po rigs dang ldan zhing brgyud kyis kyang dag pa de dag thams cu bkug nas rin po che'i mdzod bgos te/
24b5(sna tshogs): gang la yang mi slu bar byino//de ltar bgos pa de dag 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i rgyal po de la dga' ba dang mgu ba chen po lhag par skyes nas/'khor lo bsgyur ba'i rgyal po dang
24b6(sna tshogs): don mtshungs pa 'gyur to snyam ste/bdag bde par sheso//kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgyal po chos kyi bdag po rang byung gis kyang sras de dag
24b7(sna tshogs): bsdus nas chos rin po che'i mdzod 'di mnyam par bgos te/sras de dag gang la yang mi slu bas de dag nga la dag dang mgu gus pa cher bskyed cing don mthun pa sangs rgyas
25a1(sna tshogs): kyi rigs mi gcod par gnas//kun dga' bo sems can gzhan dman pA lnga mos pa nga rgyal can lta bu la spyod pa mtshan ma la spyod pa/dmigs pa la spyod pa
25a2(sna tshogs): ngo'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal gyis bcom pa/'dod chags dang /zhe sdang dang /gti mug gi zil gyis gnon pa/log po'i lam du dong bya rnams kyis chos rin po che 'di bzod
25a3(sna tshogs): par mi nuso//kun dga' bo dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams ni 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i nor mi 'dod kyi/kun dga' bo gang dag 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i bur gyur pa de dag ni
25a4(sna tshogs): 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i nor 'dod de//kun dga' bo sems can dbul po rnams ni 'khor lo rin po che dang /glang po rin po che dang /rta rin po che dang /nor bu rin po che dang /
25a5(sna tshogs): bud med rin po che dang /khyim bdag rin po che dang /blon po rin po che dang /gos mang po dang /gser dang /nor bu dang /mu tig dang /bai DUr+ya dang /dung dang /man shel
25a6(sna tshogs): dang /byi ru dang /sa la sbom dang /dngul mang po dag dgos par mi 'dzin te/rnyed kyang dga' bar kun tu spyod par mi nus shing /rin thang chung ngur 'tshong la mi mkhas pasa?
25a7(sna tshogs): 'dor ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/de dag rin po che la mi mkhas pa'i phyir//kun dga' bo sems can dbul po ni rin po che 'di'i ming ni 'di'o zhes bya bar rin po che rnams kyi ming
25b1(sna tshogs): yang mo she sau//kun dga' bo dro bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras bden pa mthong ba rnams dang /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag ni chos rin po che'i mdzod 'di tshol/
25b2(sna tshogs): ba ste/chos rin po che mig su med pa/stong pa nyid dang ldan pa/sangs rgyas kyi chos dang ldan pa 'di 'dod cing bzod/de dag des bya ba byed//sems can dbul po thos pa dang //
25b3(sna tshogs): bral ba thos pa nyams pa mig dang mi ldan pa'i byis pa de dag ni chos rin po che'o mdzod rnyed kyang ci zhig bya zhes 'dor zhing gzhan la sbyin par somaso//kun dga' bo gdil pa dang
25b4(sna tshogs): g.yung po dang /sgyu ma mkhan dang /dbul pos 'tsho ba'i sems can gang gzhan la las rin po che mang po rnyed na bdag ma spyod de rin 'chu ngur 'tshong zhing 'dor ro//kun dga' bo
25b5(sna tshogs): sems can dbul po zhes bya ba de ni mu stegs can thams cad dang /gang mu stegs can gyi nyan thos rnams kyi tshig bla dag so//kun dga' bo sems can dbul po zhes bya ba de ni/
25b6(sna tshogs): byis pa so so'i skye bo lta bu'i 'dam du bying ba dmigs pa can 'ching ba la mngon par zhen pa/mtshan ma la spyod pa/lam log par song ba rnams kyi tshig bla dgas te/
25b7(sna tshogs): ngag ni chos rin po che 'di rnyed na kun du spyod mi nus shing 'dor te don med par yang gzhan la yang sbyin par byed de/kun dga' bo gang sangs rgyas kyi sras sangs rgyas kyi spyod
26a1(sna tshogs): yul la spyod pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rgyun mi gcad par gnas pa de dag chos rin po che 'di la yongasu spyod do//rnyed nus kyang chud mi gson cing 'di/
26a2(sna tshogs): la rin po cher 'du shes por 'gyur ro//kun dga' bo was ni sring ge'i sgra sgrogs mi nuso//kun dga' bo gang seng ge'i phrug gur gyur la seng ge chen pos bskyed pa de
26a3(sna tshogs): dag seng ge'i sgra sgro gso//kun dga' bo de bzhin du wa lta bu ni byis pa so so'i skye bo log par lta ba thams cad de/de dag gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i sgra dang
26a4(sna tshogs): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas seng ge'i chen po'i chos yongasu longs spyod par mi nus//kun dga' bo gang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sras sangs rgyas kyi//
26a5(sna tshogs): seng ge chen po dang /rang byung gi ye shes kyis bskyed pa dag ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi seng ge'i sgra sgrogs shing kun tu spyod do//de nas bcom ldan 'das/
26a6(sna tshogs): la tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to//bcom ldan 'das 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor yongasu dag po 'di ni ngo mtshar lagaso//bcom
26a7(sna tshogs): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor/rang byung gi 'khor/mi tshugs pa'i 'khor/rdo rje lta bu'i 'khor/mi bskul mi bskyod pa/mi 'khrug pa'i 'khor yong
26b1(sna tshogs): su dag pa 'di ni rab tu ngo mtshor lagaso//de skad ces gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to//shA ri'i bu khyod 'khor
26b2(sna tshogs): 'di'i ston yongasu brjod dam/gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das bdag gis 'khor 'di'i ston yong su brjod lnga rngo mi thog lag so//de ci'i skab ni na/bcom ldan 'das 'khor 'di
26b3(sna tshogs): ni ri rab dang 'dra ste/ston mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa legs pa'i sladu'o//ka' stsal pa/shA ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin te/'khor 'di ni ston mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa ste/
26b4(sna tshogs): 'khor 'di'i yin gyi mtha' yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang rtogs par mi nus ni/sems can gzhan thams cad kyis lta ci smos/shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin
26b5(sna tshogs): gshegs pas bslus pa ma yin zhing /'di la de bzhin gshegs pas rtsol ba ci yang mi mdzad/rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas nga'i ming thos nas 'khor 'dir 'dus te de bzhin gaH
26b6(sna tshogs): pa'i 'khor 'dri gang la yang ma glengs ma bsgo bar de dag rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas bskul nas 'khor 'dir lhag so//'di lta bu'i chos bstan pa la 'di lta bu'i sems can chen po 'ang
26b7(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur ba ni de'i chos nyid//shA ra dwa ti'i bu gang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gzhan dag byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod the tshom thams cad gcod pa 'di yang dag par ston to//
27a1(sna tshogs): de dag gu 'khor kyang 'di lta bur 'du bar 'gyur te/'di lta bu 'di dran pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gdon mi za ba 'byung ba ni chos bstan pa 'di chos nyid//dun/
27a2(sna tshogs): dga' bo'i le'u zhes bya ste/gnyis pa'o////de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la bka'
27a3(sna tshogs): pa/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba la byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang zhe na/
27a4(sna tshogs): gang chos thams cad kyi tshu rol rtogs pa ste/de ni bstan par mi nus mod kyi ji ltar khyed shes par 'gyur ba dang /ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tha snod kyi tshig tu
27a5(sna tshogs): ba de ltar rab tu bshad par bya'o//gzugs shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin te/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gzugs las gzhan po yang ma yin//de bzhin
27a6(sna tshogs): du sbyar te de ltar tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin te/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par
27a7(sna tshogs): shes pa las gzhan pa yang ma yin no//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs kyi pho rol gang yin pa de gzugs ma yin la de bzhin du sbyar
27b1(sna tshogs): te/de ltar tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i pha rol gang yin pa de rnam par shes pa ma yin pa'i phyir//gzugs kyi pha rol ji lta bar
27b2(sna tshogs): gzugs kyang de bzhin no//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar rnam par shes pa yang de bzhino/rnam
27b3(sna tshogs): par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhino//chos thams cad kyi pha rol gang yin pa de dag ni chos thams cad ma yin//chos thams cad kyi pha rol ji lta
27b4(sna tshogs): bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhi no//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de la gzugs kyi pha rol gang yin pa de gzugs ma yino zhes khya ba de ni gzugs kyi rang bzhin bstan
27b5(sna tshogs): pa'o//gzugs kyi pha rol ji lta bar gzugs kyang de bzhin no zhes bya ba de ni gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid bshad pa bstan pa'o//de ni gzugs kyi ji lta ba bzhin bstan pa'o//de ni
27b6(sna tshogs): gzugs kyi rang bzhin bstan pa'o//de ni gzugs kyi mi dmigs po bstan pa'o//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i pha
27b7(sna tshogs): la gang yin pa de rnam par shes pa ma yin no zhes bya ba de ni rnam par shes pa'i 'bral ba bstan pa'o//rnam par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar rnam par shes pa yang de bzhin//
28a1(sna tshogs): zhes bya ba de ni rnam par shes pa'i ngo bo nyid bshad po bstan pa'o//de ni rnam par shes pa'i ji lta ba bzhin dang /rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin dang rnam byang hA/
28a2(sna tshogs): pa mi dmigs pa bstan pa'i//rnam par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin zhes bya ba dang /chos thams cad kyi pha rol gang yin pa de dag chos
28a3(sna tshogs): thams cad ma yin zhes bya ba de ni chos thams cad kyi 'bral ba bstan pa'o//chos thams cad kyi pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin zhes bya ba de na chos thams cad
28a4(sna tshogs): kyi ngo bo nyid bshad pa bston pa'o//de ni chos thams cad kyi ji lta ba bzhin dang /chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang /chos thams cad mi dmigs pa bstan pa'o//
28a5(sna tshogs): chos thams cad kyi ji lta ba bzhin dang /chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang /chos thams cad kyi mi dmigs pa ji lta bar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang de bzhin te/
28a6(sna tshogs): rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzugs la mi gnaso//tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes
28a7(sna tshogs): pa la mi gnas//shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzugs kyi nang ngam/phyi 'am/gnyi ga med pa las ring du gnas pa yang ma yin te/tshor ba dang /'du shes
28b1(sna tshogs): dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i nang ngam/phyi 'am/gnyi ga med pa las ring du gnas pa ma yin//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa shes rab kyi phar/
28b2(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa ni gzugs dang ldan pa yang ma yin/gzugs dang mi ldan pa yang mA yin//shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /
28b3(sna tshogs): rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa yang ma yin/mi ldan pa yang ma yin//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni chos gang dang yang ldan pa yang
28b4(sna tshogs): ma yin mi ldan pa yang ma yino//gzugs kyi de bzhin nyid dang /ma nor pa de bzhin nyid dang /gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid dang /ji lta ba bzhin gyi de bzhin nyid gang
28b5(sna tshogs): yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa'i de bzhin nyid dang /ma nor pa de bzhin nyid dang /
28b6(sna tshogs): gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid dang /ji lta ba bzhin gyi de bzhin nyid gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gzugs shes bya
28b7(sna tshogs): ba'adi ni gzugs dang bral ba'o//de ci'i phyir zhe na/gzugs la ni gzugs med/gang med pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du
29a1(sna tshogs): byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang de bzhin te/rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba 'di ni rnam par shes pa dang /
29a2(sna tshogs): bral ba'o//rnam par shes pa la rnam par shes pa med/gang med pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gzugs ni
29a3(sna tshogs): gzugs kyi rang bzhin dang bral ba'o//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin dang
29a4(sna tshogs): bral ba ste/bral ba'i rang bzhin gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//gzugs la gzugs kyi rang bzhin mdo//tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams
29a5(sna tshogs): dang /rnam par shes pa la rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin med/rang bzhin med pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
29a6(sna tshogs): gzugs ni gzugs kyi spyod yul ma yino//tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes po yang rnam par shes pa'i spyod yul ma yino//
29a7(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa spyod yul ma yin zhes bya ba ni gzugs kyis gzugs yang dag par mi shes mi mthong ba ste/gzugs kyis mi shes mi mthong ba
29b1(sna tshogs): gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pas rnam par shes pa mi
29b2(sna tshogs): shes mi mthong ngo //rnam par shes pas mi shes mi mthong ba gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa gzu kyi gzu kyi de nyid mi shes
29b3(sna tshogs): tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pas rnam par shes pa'i ngo bo nyid mi shes te/ngo bo nyid med par yongasu shes pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
29b4(sna tshogs): pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni gzugs la kun tu sbyor bar mi byed kun tu mi sbyor bar yang ma yin no//tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed
29b5(sna tshogs): rnams dang /rnam par shes pa ni rnam par shes pa la kun du sbyor bar yang mi byed/kun tu mi sbyor bar yang mi byed de//gzugs dang /tshor ba
29b6(sna tshogs): dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa kun tu sbyor bar yang mi byed kun tu mi sbyor bar yang mi byed pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//
29b7(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni 'bri bar 'gyur ba 'am/'phel bar 'gyur ba ma yin//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang
30a1(sna tshogs): rnam par shes pa yang 'bri bar 'gyur ba 'am/'phol bar 'gyur ba ma yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /
30a2(sna tshogs): rnam par shes pa ma 'bri mi 'phel ba gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba 'am
30a3(sna tshogs): rnam par byung bar 'gyur ba ma yin//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba 'am/rnam
30a4(sna tshogs): par byung bar 'gyur ba ma yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa kun nas nyon mongs pa ma yin/rnam par bya/
30a5(sna tshogs): ba ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni rnam par dag pa'i chos can yang ma yin/rnam par
30a6(sna tshogs): ma dag pa'i chos can yang ma yin//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang rnam par dag pa'i chos can snang mi snyan
30a7(sna tshogs): rnam par ma dag pa'i chos can yang ma yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa rnam par dag pa'i chog nyid
30b1(sna tshogs): kyang ma yin rnam par ma dag pa'i chos nyid kyang ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni 'phyo ba 'am/ma 'pho bam
30b2(sna tshogs): yon//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang 'pho ba 'am/mi 'pho ba mAM yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /
30b3(sna tshogs): 'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa 'phro ba yang ma yin mi 'pho ba yang ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs
30b4(sna tshogs): ni sbyor ba'am/mi sbyor ba ma yin no//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang sbyor ba 'am mi sbyor ba ma yin te/gzugs dang //
30b5(sna tshogs): tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa 'dra ba yang mye yini 'bral ba yang me yin pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rdul
30b6(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa/gzugs ni 'chi 'pho 'am skye ba ma yin//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa yang 'chi 'pho dang skye
30b7(sna tshogs): ma yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa 'chi 'pho ba yang ma yin/skye ba ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes rab kyi
31a1(sna tshogs): rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsalA gyis rnam par gnon pa gzugs ni skye ba 'am 'tsho ba ma yino//de bzhin du tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams
31a2(sna tshogs): dradang /rnam par shes pa yod skye ba 'am 'chi ba ma yin te/gzugs dang /tshor ba dang /'du shes dang /'du byed rnams dang /rnam par shes pa ni mi skye mo 'chi ba ga
31a3(sna tshogs): yin pa de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o//rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/gzugs ni 'khor bar 'gyur ba 'am/'khor ba'i chos can ma yin no//de bzhin du
